    $(function () {
        var imageInterval;
        var textInterval;

        function DoSlideshow() {
            $('.slideshow-image:gt(0)').hide();
            imageInterval = setInterval(function () {
                $('.slideshow-image:first-child').fadeOut(10).next('.slideshow-image').fadeIn(500).end().appendTo('.slideshow-images');
            }, 3000);
        }


        $('#slideshow-prev').click(function (event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            if (!$(".slideshow-image").is(':animated')) {
                clearInterval(imageInterval);
                clearInterval(textInterval);
                $('.slideshow-image:first-child').fadeOut(10).end();
                $('.slideshow-image:last-child').fadeIn(10).end();
                $('.slideshow-image:first-child').appendTo('.slideshow-images').end();
                // if you have 2 or less images, comment out the next 2 lines
                $('.slideshow-image:first-child').fadeOut(10).next('.slideshow-image').fadeIn(10).end().appendTo('.slideshow-images');
                //jlin 2013 09 30
                //$('.slideshow-image:first-child').fadeOut(1000).prev('.slideshow-image').fadeIn(1000).end().appendTo('.slideshow-images');
                //$('.banner-top-content:first-child').fadeOut(0).prev('.banner-top-content').fadeIn(0).end().appendTo('.slideshow-text');
                DoSlideshow();
            }
        });

        $('#slideshow-next').click(function (event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            if (!$(".slideshow-image").is(':animated')) {
                clearInterval(imageInterval);
                clearInterval(textInterval);
                $('.slideshow-image:first-child').fadeOut(10).next('.slideshow-image').fadeIn(1000).end().appendTo('.slideshow-images');
                DoSlideshow();
            }
        });
        DoSlideshow();
    });
    
',

    function windowpop(url, width, height) {
        var leftPosition, topPosition;
        //Allow for borders.
        leftPosition = (window.screen.width / 2) - ((width / 2) + 10);
        //Allow for title and status bars.
        topPosition = (window.screen.height / 2) - ((height / 2) + 50);
        //Open the window.
        window.open(url, "Window2", "status=no,height=" + height + ",width=" + width + ",resizable=no,left=" + leftPosition + ",top=" + topPosition + ",screenX=" + leftPosition + ",screenY=" + topPosition + ",toolbar=no,menubar=no,scrollbars=yes,location=no,directories=no");

    $(function () {
        var imageInterval;
        var textInterval;

        function DoSlideshow() {
            $('.slideshow-image:gt(0)').hide();
            imageInterval = setInterval(function () {
                $('.slideshow-image:first-child').fadeOut(10).next('.slideshow-image').fadeIn(500).end().appendTo('.slideshow-images');
            }, 3000);
        }


        $('#slideshow-prev').click(function (event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            if (!$(".slideshow-image").is(':animated')) {
                clearInterval(imageInterval);
                clearInterval(textInterval);
                $('.slideshow-image:first-child').fadeOut(10).end();
                $('.slideshow-image:last-child').fadeIn(10).end();
                $('.slideshow-image:first-child').appendTo('.slideshow-images').end();
                // if you have 2 or less images, comment out the next 2 lines
                $('.slideshow-image:first-child').fadeOut(10).next('.slideshow-image').fadeIn(10).end().appendTo('.slideshow-images');
                //jlin 2013 09 30
                //$('.slideshow-image:first-child').fadeOut(1000).prev('.slideshow-image').fadeIn(1000).end().appendTo('.slideshow-images');
                //$('.banner-top-content:first-child').fadeOut(0).prev('.banner-top-content').fadeIn(0).end().appendTo('.slideshow-text');
                DoSlideshow();
            }
        });

        $('#slideshow-next').click(function (event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            if (!$(".slideshow-image").is(':animated')) {
                clearInterval(imageInterval);
                clearInterval(textInterval);
                $('.slideshow-image:first-child').fadeOut(10).next('.slideshow-image').fadeIn(1000).end().appendTo('.slideshow-images');
                DoSlideshow();
            }
        });
        DoSlideshow();
    });
    
',
